NOTICE 1837-1839

NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICE
Mr. M. Veeraiah was born as a male Child of V. Mariappan on 30th June 1990 residing at No. VMMK 292, Railway
Peder Road, Aravanigal Nala Maiyam, Virudhunagar. After an elaborate sexual reassignment surgery she has been living
as a female (Reference Dr. V. Jayaraman, MS, Mch, MNAMS, Dip,NB,Phd, FICS, Professor Head Department of Burns,
Plastic & Reconstructive surgery, Kilpauk Medical College Hospital, Chennai-600 010). The through clinical Examination
under Dr. V. Jayaraman, MS, Mch, MNAMS, Dip,NB,Phd, FICS, shows that I could be treated as a female, M. Veeraiah shall
be known as M. SARATHA.
Virudhunagar,
16th August 2013.

ON BEHALF OF THE GOVERNMENT OF TAMIL NADU

M. VEERAIAH.
